 ' Eminent writer and retired IPS officer Vibhuti Narayan said on Saturday that the then government had not taken appropriate action in the massacre case in Hashimpura, Meerut 28 years ago, fearing rebellion by the PAC force
 unhone kaha, uske baad ai tathakthith dharmanirpekshatavaadi sarkaron ne bhi peediton ko nyaay dilaane ke liye koi gambheer pahal karne ke bajaay maamle ko dabaane kii koshish kii
 Rai said in a lecture organized by the Milat Bedari Campaign Committee (MBMC) at the Maulana Azad Library, Aligarh Muslim University, that the massacre of more than 40 Muslims in Hashimpura, Meerut, on May 22, 1987, took place in the country
 Is the biggest event
 ise kabhi bhulaayaa nahin ja saktaa
 He said that in a recent judgment by a Delhi court, the victims of the Hashimpura case did not get justice because the previous investigation in this case was half-completed
 raay ne kaha ki jis vakt hashimpura cond hua, us vakt vah meerut main ipies adhikari kii haisiyat se ek varisht pad par the
 In the meeting of senior police officers after that incident, he had spoken of taking immediate action against the officers and soldiers of the PAC, against whom prima facie evidence of involvement in that mass murder was clearly evident
 unhone kaha, 'us vakt mujhase kaha gaya ki agar karrwai kii gai to piesi bal vidroh kar degaa
 Then i said that if the PAC rebels, the army will be called to deal with it, because if action is not taken against the culprits, it will be a threat to justice
 uske 24 ghante ke andar vah cese mere haathon se le liya gaya or siaidi ke supurd kar diya gaya
 What happened after that is history
 ' Rai said that it was even more shocking that many governments followed in Uttar Pradesh
 unamem se kai sarkarein to samaajawaadee party (sapa) samet un dalon yaa gathbandhanon kii thim, jo khud ko dharmanirpekshata kaa almbardaar kehete the, lekin ve sarkarein hashimpura cond ke peediton ko nyaay dilaanaa to dur, maamle ko dabaane ke liye sakriy rup se shaamil raheen
 The retired IPS said that when the Hashimpura incident took place, both the Center and the state had a Congress government at that time
 ve donon hi sarkarein isi jugat main dikhin ki peediton ko nyaay naa mili
 He said that the media also failed to bring out the truth
 chaahe vah vaardaat ke vakt kii baat ho yaa phir uske baad kii

 main ise naa likhane ko lekar baari dabaav main tha, kyonki log aisi syah ghatnaon ko bhul janaa chaahate hai

 yah jaankaree ek media rapat se mili
 According to the government newspaper 'to Vima', both sides have agreed to the 2015 deficit and the excesses of 2016 and 2017 and have ruled out any new move for 2015-16
 samjhauta subah 8 baje ke baad hua
 The talks had been going on since Monday morning
 18 ghante kii is marathon vaarta main greece sarkaar kii ore se vitt mantri euclid sacalotose or aarthik mantri jeeorgos stethakis hissaa le rahe the
 According to government sources, the negotiations led to agreements on disputed issues like new privatization funds, deregulation of energy and non-performing loans
 is samjhaute ke tahat sarkaar ko turant 35 kadam uthaane honge
 Steps to be taken under the agreement include changes in tax structure for shipping companies, lowering prices of generic medicines, review of social welfare system, strengthening of the Financial Crimes Prevention Squad (SDOE), relinquishing the first retirement program, islands by 2016 To abolish tax exemption, implement product market reforms proposed by the Organization for Economic Co-operation and Development (OECD), and the Energy Eagle And measures such as free from regulation are mainly involved
 iske saath hi nijee adhyaapan mulya vardhit kar (waite) badhaakar 23 fisadi kiya jayega or bif par waite kii dar 23 fisadi se ghataakar 13 fisadi kii jaaegi
 The comments greece ke samachar patr kathimerini ke mutabik yadi samjhauta puraa hota he, to greece sansad main is par guuruuvaar ko matdaan hoga

 The settlement took place after 8 am
 vaarta somvaar subah se chal rahi thi

 Nevertheless, the effect of economic policies is definitely indicated by the economic growth rate
 yadi videsh niti ke saidhantik pahalu ko nikaal diya jaae to videsh vyapaar yani niryaat-aayaat pradarshan se kisi sarkaar kii videsh niti kii safalataa ko napa ja saktaa he, kyonki dwipaksheeya vyapaar or puunji kii awajahi kisi desh ke global kootnithik rishton kii buniyaad he
 The formula for concretely measuring the success of foreign policy might be to look at preferential trade agreements with various countries under a government, because the more agreements, the more foreign trade
 yah formula hamane nahin, 2015-16 kii aarthik samiksha ne diya he jo videsh niti kii safalataa ko parakhane kaa ek nayaa paimaana sujhaati he
 Now that the grand diplomatic campaigns of the Modi government have sunk and India's exports are reeling from their longest recession, the criterion of this formula of economic review is reflected in the foreign policy questions of the Modi government
 darasal, beete baras jab pradhanmantri neuyork, sidney yaa wemble ke stadimon main anivaasiyon se samvaad kar rahe the, thik usee samay unki sarkaar ke roodhiwaadee aagrah bharat ke videsh vyapaar main udaarikaran kii koshishon ko shradhanjali de rahe the or mukt va variyak vyapaar sandhiyon ko roak rahe the jo taaja adhyayanon main bharat kii vyapaarik safalataa kaa aadhaar banakar ubhare hai
 In August last year, due to indigenous pressures and aggressive insistence on the FTA, the government halted negotiations on the European Union Free Trade Treaty (india-eu FTA), which is considered India's most ambitious FTA after ASEAN
 aarthik samiksha kii roshni main pat kii vyavastha ke bharat ke videsh vyapaar par asar kii thos va tathyaparak padtaal kii ja sakati he
 a point-finding conclusion of this investigation is that the total trade between 2010 and 2014 with countries with which India has entered into a two-way or multilateral free or preferential trade agreement (FTA / PTA) increased by 50 per cent
 vajahah pat / pitie main shaamil desh duusare desh se hone vaale aayaat ke liye custom duty main kami karte hai or vyapaar pratibandhon ko simit karte hai jiskaa sidhaa asar vyapaar main badhat ke taur par saamne aata he
 There are three types of models active on trade agreements in the world
 pehla varg dablutio, trans pacific partnership (tipipi) jaisi bahupaksheeya vyapaar sandhiyon kaa he
 The WTO was not very successful, while the land of TPP is still being prepared
 doosraa varg kshetreey trade block asian (dakshin-purv asian deshon kaa sanghathan), nafta (uttar america), iyu (europea samudaay) kaa he jo kshetreey vyapaar badhaane main kaaphi safal rahe hai
 The third category is of ftas which have emerged as the most important means of increasing trade and investment in the world
 inamen deshon ke bich dwipaksheeya samjhaute or trade block ke saath samjhaute shaamil hai
 India is far behind in this competition
 bharat ne pat kii shuruyaat 1970 main india africa trade agreement ke saath kii thi lekin 2010 tak keval 19 pat ho paae hai jabaki vishwa main 2004 se lekar 2014 tak har saal ausatan 15 pat hue hai, bich ke kuch varshon main to inaki sankhya 20 or 25 se upar rahi he
 Most of India's ftas are in Asia
 asia se baahar do pat marcosur (brazil, argentina, urugve, paragway, venezuela) or chile ke saath hai
 India's most important ftas in Asia are with ASEAN, Korea and Japan based on trade volume
 aarthik samiksha ke mutabik, in deshon ke saath pat hone ke baad bharat ke vyapaar main 50 fisadi kii badhotaree hui he
 Prior to the FTA with countries other than these countries with which India has ftas, India's export growth during 2007 to 2014 was 13 per cent, which increased to 22 per cent after FTA, which was the success of free trade agreements
 Is proof asian ke saath bharat kaa pat (2010) sabase safal mana jaataa he
 The latest figures suggest that India's exports to ASEAN countries increased by 25 per cent in the four years to 2014, up from 14 per cent before the FTA
 aayaat main badhotaree 19 fisadi rahi jo pat se pehle 13 fisadi thi
 After the success of ASEAN, expectations regarding FTA between India and the European Union were very high as Europe is the second largest market in the world and new energy in Indian exports is necessary to enter this market
 lekin afsos ki modi sarkaar ke asamanjas or roodhiwaadita ke chalate yah mahatvapurn pahal jahaan kii tahaan thahar gai
 As a result, India's summit with the EU was held in Brussels this week, but no talk was made on the most important agenda, the FTA, and the whole event became an event diplomacy
 yadi aarthik samiksha sahi he to swadeshi pongapathi ke dabaav main iyu pat ko rokna sarkaar kii galati he
 In fact, not stopping any kind of preferential trade agreements or taking initiatives on their behalf is a major diplomatic lapse that the government has made repeatedly in the last two years
 bharat kaa niryaat aaj agar 15 maah ke nunatam str par he to shaayad isaki ek badi vajah yah bhi he ki sangrakshanvaadi agrahon ke chalate modi sarkaar ne mukt bazaar samjhauton kii raftaar tej nahin kii
 The Prime Minister has to understand that the success of foreign trade of any country now depends on preferential trade agreements and these agreements come out of diplomatic campaigns
 unke kootnithik abhiyaanon kaa jaadu isliye utarane laga he kyonki unki diplomasi main mukt or udaar bazaar kii chetana nadaarad he

 vardhman ne kareeb chah maheene baad phir se ladaaku vimaan udaaya he
 In fact, on 27 February, his plane was dropped during an air duel between India and Pakistan and he was injured while leaving the plane
 sena ke sheersh adhikari ne bataaya, 'unhone (vardhman ne) vimaan udaana shuru kar diya he
 Currently, Vardhman is serving at an Indian Air Force base in Rajasthan
 '36 saal ke payalat ne pakistani vimaanon ke saath aasmaan main hui ladaai main apane mig 21 bison vimaan se pakistan kaa atyaadhunik vimaan epa-16 maar giraaya tha
 After this, his mig-21 was killed
 vah vimaan se surakshit nikal gaye the lekin parachute se pakistani ilaake main utre the jahaan unhen pakistani sena ne pakad liya tha

 mig 21 vimaan se nikalne ke dauraan vah chotil ho gaye the

 iske liye CRPF kii helpline madadgaar he

 saath hi surakshabalon ke saamne sarender kar diya

 India may get a new building for the Parliament House equipped with state-of-the-art technology, which has been proposed by Lok Sabha Speaker Sumitra Mahajan
 adhyaksh ne kaha he ki vartmaan 88 saal puraani imaarat par badhati umr kaa asar dikhne laga he or yah adhik jagah kii badhati maang ko puraa karne main ab sakasham nahin he
 Sources said that Mahajan has written a letter to Urban Development Minister m Venkaiah Naidu regarding this and asked him to consider starting the construction work of the new Parliament House complex
 iske liye do vaikalpik sthal sujhaayen hai
 
 ek sansad bhawan parisar main hi or doosraa sameep hi rajpath ke us sthaan par jahaan raksha or dilli police ke kuch barrack sthit hai
 Sources said that as per the letter to the Ministry of Urban Development, there is a possibility that the ministry will prepare a note for the cabinet where it can be considered
 apane patr main sumitra mahajan ne likhaa he ki saal 2026 ke baad loksabhaa ke siton kii sankhya badhane kii sambhaavna he or yah samvidhan ke anuchhed 81 ke upbandh 3 ke tahat ho saktaa he
 Currently the seating capacity in the Lok Sabha is 550 seats and cannot be increased
 is anuchhed ke tahat 2026 main 2021 kii sambhavit janaganana ke anuroop pratinidhitiv kii sankhya ko phir se tay kiya ja saktaa he
 Justifying the need for a new building for Parliament, Sumitra Mahajan said that when the present building was taken into service in 1927, the number of employees, security personnel, media, people visiting Parliament was limited but in these years here The number of visitors has increased manifold
 venkaiya naidu ko likhe patr main sumitra mahajan ne kaha, ‘sansad ke vartmaan bhawan kii umr or kaaryon evam karmchaariyon kii sankhya badhane or uske zyada istemaal kii vajah se is par asar pad rahaa he
 The speaker wrote, "under these circumstances, the construction of a new state-of-the-art building of Parliament is needed
 ’ unhone yah bhi kaha ki sansad kaa vartmaan bhawan 88 varsh purana ho gaya he
 The Lok Sabha Speaker said that earlier this building was only for mps and Secretariat staff
 lekin sansadeey kaamkaaj badhane, samitiyon or suraksha jarurate badhane ke kaaran jagah kii maang kai guna bad gai he
 The Speaker said that since the Parliament building has been declared as 'heritage Site Grade 1', there are several limitations in the repair, expansion, alteration and alteration of its structure
 loksabhaa adhyaksh ne likhaa ki agar sansad bhawan ke kendriya kaksh ko bhi loksabhaa chambar ke rup main badla jaae tab bhi 550 sadasyon se adhik isamen nahin aa sakenge
 Currently, the central hall has a capacity of 398 seats
 sumitra mahajan ne kaha ki praudyogiki ke lagaataar unnat hone ke bich aisi yojana he ki saansadon ko atyaadhunik upkarnon se las kiya jaae or sansad ko kagaji karrwai se mukt kiya jaae
 He said that due to this, the system of meeting in the Lok Sabha Chamber will need to be redesigned
 chambar main vartmaan baithne kii vyavastha kii simaaen hai, nayi imaarat se atyaadhunik praudyogiki se las aadhunik sansad kaa vikalp pesh hoga
 Sumitra Mahajan wrote that one option for the construction of the new Parliament House would be within the campus itself and the other could be on the other side of Rajpath which is a suitably large area and where there could be freedom to design the new complex
 tippaniyan Both the existing building and the proposed new building complexes have also been suggested to be connected by underground

 In his letter, Sumitra Mahajan has written that the number of Lok Sabha seats is likely to increase after the year 2026 and this can be done under clause 3 of Article 81 of the Constitution
 abhi loksabhaa main baithne kii kshamta 550 siton kii he or ise badhaayaa nahin ja saktaa he
 Under this Article, the number of representation can be rescheduled to correspond to a possible census of 2021 in 2026

 In a letter to Venkaiah Naidu, Sumitra Mahajan said, 'it is impacting due to the age and functions of the present House of Parliament and the increasing number of staff and its use
 ’ spikar ne likhaa, ‘in paristhitiyon main sansad ke naye atyaadhunik imaarat ke nirmaan kii jarurat he

 loksabhaa adhyaksh ne kaha ki pehle yah bhawan keval saansadon or sachivalay ke karmchaariyon ke liye tha

 adhyaksh ne kaha ki chunki sansad kii imaarat ko ‘dharohar sthal grad 1’ ghoshit kiya gaya he, iske dhaanche kii marammat, isamen vistaar, badlaav or parivartan main kai tarah kii simaaen he
 The Lok Sabha Speaker wrote that even if the Central Hall of the Parliament House is also converted into a Lok Sabha Chamber, more than 550 members will not be able to come to it
 abhi kendriya kaksh kii kshamta 398 siton kii he
 Sumitra Mahajan said that with the continuous advancement of technology, there is a plan that mps should be equipped with state-of-the-art equipment and Parliament should be exempted from paperwork
 unhone kaha ki iske kaaran loksabhaa chambar main baithak kii vyavastha ko nae sire se taiyaar karne kii jarurat hogi
 The chamber has limitations of the current seating arrangement, the new building will offer an alternative to a modern parliament equipped with state-of-the-art technology
